# math.SG [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Lagrangian capacity and chain level string topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20051)
*Shah Faisal,Yin Li*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文推导了具有有限Gutt-Hutchings容量的Liouville域的Lagrangian容量的上界，证明任意维凸或凹环面域的Lagrangian容量等于其对角线值，完全解决了Cieliebak-Mohnke关于椭球体Lagrangian容量的猜想。证明基于Fukaya-Irie技术的S^1-等变变体，避免了局部相切约束的全纯曲线带来的横截性问题。此外，证明了n维椭球体中任何极值Lagrangian环面必须位于边界上。应用包括Liouville流形中非球面Lagrangian的Lagrangian宽度新上界，以及4维和6维中许多非次临界Weinstein域的Lagrangian容量的首次计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Cieliebak-Mohnke关于椭球体Lagrangian容量的猜想，并建立一般凸/凹环面域Lagrangian容量的精确刻画。

Method: 基于Fukaya和Irie技术的S^1-等变变体，不依赖具有局部相切约束的全纯曲线，从而避免横截性问题。

Result: (1) 导出了Liouville域Lagrangian容量的上界；(2) 证明了凸或凹环面域的Lagrangian容量等于其对角线；(3) 证明了椭球体中极值Lagrangian环面必在边界上；(4) 给出了非球面Lagrangian的宽度新上界；(5) 首次计算了若干非次临界Weinstein域的Lagrangian容量。

Conclusion: 完全解决了Cieliebak-Mohnke猜想，并为更一般Weinstein域的Lagrangian容量计算提供了新工具。

Abstract: We derive upper bounds for the Lagrangian capacities of Liouville domains with finite Gutt--Hutchings capacities and show that the Lagrangian capacity of a convex or concave toric domain of arbitrary dimension equals its diagonal. In particular, this completely settles the conjecture of Cieliebak-Mohnke on the Lagrangian capacity of ellipsoids. Our proof is based on an $S^1$-equivariant variant of the techniques of Fukaya and Irie, and does not use holomorphic curves with local tangency constraints, which would inevitably cause transversality issues. Moreover, we show that any extremal Lagrangian torus in an $n$-dimensional ellipsoid must lie on the boundary. Applications of our results and techniques include new upper bounds on the Lagrangian width for aspherical Lagrangians in Liouville manifolds and the first computations of the Lagrangian capacities for many non-subcritical Weinstein domains in dimensions 4 and 6.

</details>


### [2] [Fourier-Helgason transform as infinite geodesic time limit in geometric quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20290)
*Ana Cristina Ferreira,Joachim Hilgert,José M. Mourão,João P. Nunes*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入量子测地线变换（QGT），解决了非紧对称空间上Fourier-Helgason变换与几何量子化之间长期存在的不一致问题，证明了在非复李群情况下，QGT的无穷时间极限（模Harish-Chandra c-函数的相位）恰好等于FH变换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lisiecki（1987）对复李群给出了FH变换的几何量子化解释，但发现对于非复李群，水平极化的Blattner-Kostant-Sternberg（BKS）配对与FH变换不等价且非酉。本文旨在解决这一长期存在的理论不一致性。

Method: 首先证明水平极化是测地流作用下垂直极化的无穷时间极限；然后将测地流提升到量子丛上的交织酉平行输运，称为量子测地线变换（QGT）；最后证明QGT在测地时间趋于无穷时存在良好定义的极限。

Result: 证明了QGT的无穷时间极限（模Harish-Chandra c-函数的相位和一个无关乘法常数）等于Fourier-Helgason变换，从而将几何量子化与FH变换在非复李群情形下统一起来。

Conclusion: 通过引入量子测地线变换，成功解决了非复李群情形下几何量子化与FH变换之间的分歧，为对称空间上的调和分析提供了新的几何量子化视角。

Abstract: The Fourier-Helgason (FH) transform for a noncompact symmetric space $G/K$ establishes the direct integral decomposition of the unitary representation of $G$ on $L^2(G/K)$ into irreducible principal series representations.
  By applying techniques of geometric quantization to the symplectic manifold $T^*(G/K),$ Lisiecki in 1987 gave a geometric interpretation of the FH transform in the case when $G$ is complex. He defined for general $G$ a ''horizontal'' polarization on $T^*(G/K)$ and showed that, for complex $G$, the Blattner-Kostant-Sternberg (BKS) pairing between the Schrödinger vertical polarization Hilbert space, $L^2(G/K)$, and the Hilbert space of horizontally polarized functions coincides with the FH transform. However, in the same paper, Lisiecki showed that for noncomplex Lie groups the BKS pairing is nonequivalent to the FH transform and nonunitary in general.
  In the present paper, we resolve this discrepancy between the FH transform and geometric quantization in the case when $G$ is not complex.
  First, we show that the horizontal polarization is the infinite-time limit of the push-forward of the vertical polarization with respect to the geodesic flow for a $G$-invariant Riemannian metric. Then we lift the geodesic flow to an intertwining unitary parallel transport on the quantum bundle that we call quantum geodesic transform (QGT). Finally we show that the QGT has a well-defined limit, as the geodesic time goes to infinity, and that it is equal, up to the phase of the Harish-Chandra $c$-function and an irrelevant multiplicative constant, to the FH transform.

</details>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Bootstrapping Pion Form Factors at Large $N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19420)
*Jan Albert,Dilara Kosva,Leonardo Rastelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在large N QCD框架下对π介子形状因子进行自举研究，结合矢量流两点函数、π介子矢量形状因子和散射振幅，利用解析性、幺正性、Regge有界性和Brodsky-Farrar渐近标度律得到严格束缚，并通过输入微扰QCD紫外行为得到类SVZ唯象束缚，最终将大N格点测量与渐近自由能标联系起来，缩紧了允许的手征拉格朗日空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大N极限下将强子自举方法与QCD拉格朗日量建立规范不变的桥梁，通过局域规范不变探针约束低能形状因子系数和手征有效理论参数。

Method: 利用解析性、幺正性及Regge有界性约束谱数据，结合Brodsky-Farrar渐近标度律得到普适严格束缚；进一步输入微扰QCD紫外行为（有限标度）得到唯象SVZ型束缚，约束π介子衰变常数、电荷半径等。

Result: 得到了两类束缚：1) 基于解析性、幺正性和渐近标度律的普适严格束缚，约束低能形状因子系数；2) 基于微扰紫外输入的唯象束缚，约束π介子衰变常数，将大N格点测量转化为渐近自由能标的下界，并约束π介子电荷半径。

Conclusion: 局域规范不变探针为强子自举与微观QCD拉格朗日量之间提供了规范不变的桥梁，大N QCD中允许的手征拉格朗日量空间被显著缩紧到预期区域。

Abstract: We initiate a bootstrap study of pion form factors in large $N$ QCD. We consider the mixed system of the vector-current two-point function, the pion vector form factor, and the pion scattering amplitude in the chiral limit. At large $N$ these observables are meromorphic, with spectral data constrained by unitarity, crossing symmetry, and Regge boundedness. We obtain bounds of two kinds. The first are rigorous and universal: from analyticity, unitarity and the asymptotic Brodsky-Farrar scaling, we constrain low-energy form-factor coefficients. The second are more phenomenological, of the Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov type: feeding in the perturbative ultraviolet behavior at a finite scale lets us bound the pion decay constant, convert a large $N$ lattice measurement into a lower bound on the scale at which asymptotic freedom sets in, and constrain the pion charge radius. Combining these inputs, the space of allowed chiral Lagrangians shrinks toward the region where large $N$ QCD is expected to sit. Our results illustrate how local gauge-invariant probes provide a canonical bridge between the hadronic bootstrap and the microscopic QCD Lagrangian.

</details>


### [4] [Calabi-Yau Orientifold Hypersurfaces and their F-theory Uplifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19423)
*Bjoern Hassfeld,Jakob Moritz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 提出一种算法，从卡拉比-丘三折叠定向折返回构造椭圆纤维化卡拉比-丘四折叠（嵌入环面簇中），并利用6维自反多面体三角剖分实现，支持计算四折叠周期和七膜超势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建从 Calabi-Yau 三折叠定向折返回到其 F-理论提升（椭圆纤维化 Calabi-Yau 四折叠）的系统的、算法化的构造方法，以支持四折叠周期和七膜超势的计算。

Method: 从定向折返数据构造6维自反多面体，然后通过三角剖分生成光滑（除孤立终端奇点外）的 Calabi-Yau 四折叠，并利用镜像流形的即时构造计算四折叠周期。

Result: 成功构造多个示例，证明算法能够生成所需的 Calabi-Yau 四折叠并计算七膜超势；算法与 CYTools 集成并通过 GitHub 发布。

Conclusion: 该算法为系统研究 F-理论紧化中的超势计算提供了有效工具，且公开可用。

Abstract: We present an algorithm that constructs Calabi-Yau threefold orientifolds and their $F$-theory uplifts to elliptically-fibered Calabi-Yau fourfolds, embedded in toric varieties at codimension one and two respectively. The resulting Calabi-Yau fourfolds arise from triangulations of $6d$ reflexive polytopes -- which our method constructs from orientifold data -- and are smooth away from isolated terminal singularities. For many of our fourfolds, the construction of the mirror manifold is immediate, enabling the computation of fourfold periods, and thus the seven-brane superpotential. We present multiple examples that demonstrate these capabilities. Our algorithms work with $\mathtt{CYTools}$ and are available through a GitHub repository.

</details>


### [5] [Moduli Stabilisation for ADD and the Dark Dimension Scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19440)
*Andreas P. Braun,Michele Cicoli,Riccardo Milioli,Roberto Valandro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在IIB大型体积场景中，通过K3纤维化的Calabi-Yau三维流形实现各向异性弦紧致化，稳定了4D K3纤维的小体积和2D ℙ¹基的大体积，从而产生一个或两个大额外维度（ADD和暗维度场景），并讨论了模谱、超对称破缺及宇宙学约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为实现ADD（大额外维度）和暗维度（Dark Dimension）这两种具有一个或两个大额外维度的各向异性弦紧致化方案，并提供具体的模稳定机制。

Method: 采用IIB大型体积场景（Large Volume Scenario），考虑K3纤维化于ℙ¹基上的Calabi-Yau三维流形。通过微扰修正（弦圈和高阶导数效应）将4D K3纤维的体积稳定在较小值，同时保持2D ℙ¹基的体积呈指数级大。通过复杂结构模稳定动态变形ℙ¹基，实现Tyurin退化极限，从而产生单一的大1D循环。

Result: 提出了统一的描述框架，ADD情况作为对称的替代极限恢复。势能可产生dS真空或quintessence逃逸，但需一定调节以匹配观测宇宙常数。给出了明确的Calabi-Yau定向折纸例子，包含一致的膜设置、消蝌蚪条件和模稳定。分析了模谱及相关现象学约束（超对称破缺、宇宙学模过产生、第五力界限）。

Conclusion: 该机制能够自然地实现各向异性弦紧致化，产生一个或两个大额外维度，为ADD和暗维度场景提供了具体的弦论实现，并受到现象学约束的限制。

Abstract: We provide a moduli stabilisation mechanism for realising anisotropic string compactifications with one or two large extra dimensions, corresponding to the ADD and Dark Dimension scenarios. This is achieved within the type IIB Large Volume Scenario, where an exponentially large Calabi-Yau volume in string units can naturally generate a parametrically low Kaluza-Klein scale. Anisotropy is realised by considering a Calabi-Yau threefold which is a K3 fibration over a $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. The volume of the 4D K3 fibre is stabilised at relatively small values by perturbative corrections to the effective action, in particular string loops and higher-derivative effects, leaving an exponentially large volume of the 2D $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. We argue that complex structure moduli stabilisation can dynamically deform the $\mathbb{P}^1$ base, corresponding to a Tyurin degeneration limit where the internal geometry effectively develops a single large 1D cycle. Within a unified description, the ADD case is instead recovered as a symmetric alternative limit. The potential can feature either a dS vacuum or a quintessence runaway, although in both cases some degree of tuning is required to match the observed cosmological constant scale. We also present an explicit Calabi-Yau orientifold example with consistent brane setup, tadpole cancellation and moduli stabilisation. We analyse the resulting moduli spectrum and associated phenomenological constraints, including supersymmetry breaking, cosmological moduli overproduction and fifth force bounds.

</details>


### [6] [Membrane instantons and non-perturbative effects in $\mathrm{AdS}_{4}/\mathrm{CFT}_{3}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19467)
*Stefan A. Kurlyand*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了Freund-Rubin背景AdS₄×Y₇中的欧几里得M2膜瞬子，揭示了BPS条件与弱G₂流形上三维子流形的结合性等价，并分析了Sasaki-Einstein流形中一类特殊BPS M2膜的量子涨落与单圈配分函数，最后应用于S⁷/Zₖ和(p,q)模型几何中的瞬子计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解AdS₄×Y₇紧化背景中M2膜瞬子的BPS条件、涨落结构及其对超对称破缺和模空间稳定化的影响，特别是精确计算瞬子配分函数的动机。

Method: 利用G₂结构和Sasaki-Einstein流形的几何性质，将BPS条件转化为结合性条件；通过约化到横向椭圆复形，将单圈配分函数用等变指标表示，并应用于具体商空间几何。

Result: 发现弱G₂流形上M2膜BPS条件等价于三维子流形的结合性；在Sasaki-Einstein情形中识别出一类保持两个实内禀Killing旋量的不变M2膜；将单圈配分函数用等变指标表达，在S⁷/Zₖ中重现S³/Zₖ瞬子结果，并推广到(p,q)模型几何。

Conclusion: 建立了AdS₄×Y₇背景中M2膜瞬子的严格BPS几何刻画，提供了一种通过等变指标计算单圈配分函数的系统方法，为M理论瞬子效应和超对称破缺研究奠定基础。

Abstract: We study Euclidean M2-brane instantons in Freund-Rubin backgrounds $\mathrm{AdS}_{4}\times \mathrm{Y}_7$. For a seven-dimensional weak $G_{2}$ manifold $\mathrm{Y}_7$, we show that the BPS condition for an M2-brane wrapping a three-cycle $Σ\subset \mathrm{Y}_7$ is equivalent to the associativity condition with respect to the nearly parallel $G_{2}$-structure. When $\mathrm{Y}_7$ is Sasaki-Einstein, we identify a special class of BPS M2-branes that preserve both real internal Killing spinors and correspond to invariant three-dimensional submanifolds inheriting a Sasakian structure. We analyse the quadratic fluctuations around BPS M2-brane instantons in these backgrounds. For the special class of M2-branes in Sasaki-Einstein manifolds, the fluctuation problem reduces to transversely elliptic complexes, and the one-loop partition function can be expressed in terms of the corresponding equivariant indices. We then apply the index formula for the one-loop partition function to invariant M2-branes in $S^{7}/\mathbb{Z}_{k}$, recovering the known result for the $S^3/\mathbb{Z}_k$ instantons and discussing more general invariant BPS cycles. As a further application, we consider M2-brane instantons with $S^3$-quotient worldvolumes in the $(p,q)$-model geometry.

</details>


### [7] [Generating Function of single-centered Black Hole Index in CHL Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19479)
*Ranveer Kumar Singh*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了在一般$\mathbb{Z}_N$ CHL模型中构造单中心黑洞指数生成函数的方法，通过从四分之一BPS双荷子指数（由亚纯Siegel模形式描述）中减去双中心黑洞指数的生成函数实现，并利用CHL模型中的黑洞束缚态蜕变构造了双中心黑洞指数生成函数，同时证明了$N=2,3$情况下该生成函数的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在CHL模型中准确分离单中心黑洞与多中心黑洞的贡献，从而构造单中心黑洞指数的生成函数，以更精确地研究黑洞微观态计数。

Method: 从四分之一BPS双荷子的亚纯Siegel模形式指数中，减去通过黑洞束缚态蜕变方法构造的双中心黑洞指数生成函数，从而得到单中心黑洞指数的生成函数。

Result: 成功构造了一般$\mathbb{Z}_N$ CHL模型中单中心黑洞指数的生成函数，并证明了在$N=2,3$情况下该生成函数的收敛性。

Conclusion: 该方法有效实现了CHL模型中单中心与多中心黑洞贡献的分离，为相关黑洞微观态计数研究提供了严谨的理论框架。

Abstract: We present the construction of the generating function of single-centered black hole index in general $\mathbb{Z}_N$ CHL models. This is done by subtracting from the index of quarter BPS dyons, described by a meromorphic Siegel modular form, the generating function for the index of two-centered black holes. We use black hole bound state metamorphosis in CHL models for the construction of the generating function of two-centered black hole index. We prove the convergence of the generating function for the cases $N=2,3$.

</details>


### [8] [Operational Tube-Sector Theory of Quantum State Distinguishability Under Generalized Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19678)
*Song He*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在具有广义对称性（包括融合范畴描述的非可逆对称性）的多体系统中，建立了量子态可区分性的变分原理。标准保真度和对称性分辨诊断被揭示为更精细操作结构的粗粒化极限。通过对称性约束下的测量资源理论，可容许的物理仪器由完全正性、纠缠截断局域性、边界模协方差和序列稳定性刻画。最优测量结构由边界管代数中心唯一确定，其原始幂等元定义管扇区概率，细化了基于保真度和对称性分辨的描述。相关的管正算子值测度（POVM）是极端的，并在对称性约束下实现最优单次假设检验可区分性。该构造对融合范畴具有普适性，且独立于微观实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有保真度和对称性分辨的量子态可区分性诊断方法较为粗糙，缺乏在具有广义对称性（尤其是非可逆对称性）的多体系统中的精细操作框架。本文旨在建立一种更基础的变分原理，统一并推广现有的可区分性度量，揭示其背后的代数结构与操作约束。

Method: 采用对称性约束下的测量资源理论框架，引入边界管代数（boundary tube algebra）作为核心代数结构。通过刻画物理容许仪器应满足的四条公理（完全正性、纠缠截断局域性、边界模协方差、序列稳定性），推导出最优测量结构由边界管代数的中心唯一确定。构造管正算子值测度（tube POVM），分析其极值性质与最优性。

Result: 建立了量子态可区分性的变分原理，证明标准保真度和对称性分辨是其粗粒化极限。揭示了最优测量结构由边界管代数的中心 $Z(\mathrm{Tube}_{\mathcal{C}}(\mathcal{M}_A))$ 唯一确定，其原始幂等元定义管扇区概率。构造的管POVM是极值的，并在对称性约束下实现最优单次假设检验可区分性。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个普适的、与微观实现无关的量子态可区分性理论框架，适用于任意融合范畴描述的广义对称性（包括非可逆对称性）。该工作深化了对对称性约束下量子测量基本限制的理解，并为多体系统中量子态区分问题提供了新的代数工具和操作视角。

Abstract: A variational principle for quantum-state distinguishability is established in many-body systems with generalized symmetries, including noninvertible cases described by fusion categories. Standard fidelity and symmetry-resolved diagnostics emerge as coarse-grained limits of a more refined operational structure. When symmetry actions terminate at entanglement cuts, distinguishability is governed by boundary tube algebras within a symmetry-constrained measurement resource theory. The physically admissible instruments are characterized by complete positivity, entanglement-cut locality, boundary-module covariance, and sequential stability. The resulting optimal measurement structure is uniquely fixed by the center of the boundary tube algebra, $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{phys}} = Z\!\left(\mathrm{Tube}_{\mathcal{C}}(\mathcal{M}_A)\right)$, whose primitive idempotents define tube-sector probabilities that refine fidelity-based and symmetry-resolved descriptions. The associated tube positive-operator-valued measures (POVM) are extremal and yield optimal one-shot hypothesis-testing distinguishability under symmetry constraints. The construction is universal across fusion categories and independent of microscopic realization.

</details>


### [9] [Quantum models with the Yang-Lee phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19732)
*Erick Arguello Cruz,Grigory Tarnopolsky*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在四种1+1D量子模型中实现了PT对称变形下的Yang-Le临界点，通过态-算符对应精确计算了标度维数，并利用玻色化等方法证明这些模型均由带iφ^3相互作用的无质量玻色场描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多个不同的量子模型中系统性地实现和研究Yang-Lee相变，验证其普适性，并确认这些模型在临界点处由相同的低能有效场论（带iφ^3相互作用的自由玻色场）描述。

Method: 采用态-算符对应识别YL临界点并计算最低算符的标度维数；利用玻色化处理Schwinger模型，利用Polyakov-Hubbard变换处理其他模型；数值计算两点关联函数。

Result: 所有模型在YL临界点的标度维数与二维YL临界性的精确结果完全一致；Schwinger模型和量子钟模型中识别出无质量和有质量态；φ的两点函数随距离增长，与理论预期一致。

Conclusion: 四种不同的1+1D量子模型均在PT对称变形下实现了杨-李相变，并由相同的有效场论统一描述，验证了杨-李临界性的普适性。

Abstract: In this article, we present four different $1+1$D quantum models that realize the Yang-Lee (YL) phase transition under a deformation that preserves $PT$ symmetry. These are the antiferromagnetic Ising spin chain in transverse and longitudinal magnetic fields, the massive Schwinger model, the Blume-Capel model, and the three-state quantum clock model. Using the state-operator correspondence, we identify the YL critical point, compute the scaling dimensions of the lowest operators in each model, and find perfect agreement with the exact results for the YL criticality in two dimensions. Using bosonization for the Schwinger model and the Polyakov-Hubbard transformation for the other models, we show that in all of these quantum models the YL critical point is described, as expected, by a massless bosonic field with an $i φ^3$ interaction. In the quantum clock model, this critical field interacts with a massive bosonic field, and we identify the massless and massive states in the Hamiltonian spectrum. In addition, we numerically compute the two-point function of $φ$ at the Yang-Lee critical point and show that it grows with distance, in agreement with theoretical expectations.

Abstract: We revisit the Coleman--Weinberg monopole problem introduced by Kiselev, where radiative symmetry breaking makes the broken vacuum metastable. Rather, the same exchanged bulk particle must also appear through its shadow-basis representative. This leads to a shadow-completed OPE, with the shadow OPE coefficient fixed by the ordinary collinear coefficient through the universal shadow factor. We discuss the corresponding boundary Hilbert-space interpretation, extend this argument to gluons and gravitons, and verify the shadow exchange directly in tree-level regular celestial amplitudes, including a scalar $2\rightarrow n$ analysis and an explicit five-point example.

</details>


### [19] [Cosmological history after higher dimensional inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20486)
*Luis A. Anchordoqui,Ignatios Antoniadis,Jules Cunat*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过高维暴胀连接粒子物理与宇宙学两大层级（引力弱性与宇宙尺度）的机制，仅允许1-2个微米尺度额外维，并构建了从暴胀结束到再加热温度的宇宙演化历史，以避免早期宇宙中体引力子的过度产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决粒子物理与宇宙学中的两大层级问题——实际引力的微弱性与可观测宇宙的巨大性，通过高维暴胀用单一基本尺度统一两者，并解决额外维稳定后体引力子过度产生的问题。

Method: 提出一种暴胀后至再加热温度的宇宙学历史方案，假设额外维在暴胀结束时存在稳定化机制，确保在早期宇宙中不存在体引力子，避免其过度产生，从而连接高维暴胀时期与标准宇宙学的起始点。

Result: 该机制仅在1-2个微米尺度额外维条件下与观测到的近似标量不变原初扰动功率谱一致；所提宇宙学历史成功避免了体引力子在早期宇宙的过度产生。

Conclusion: 所提出的宇宙学历史有效填补了高维暴胀结束到标准宇宙学开始之间的空白，为额外维稳定化后的早期宇宙演化提供了自洽描述。

Abstract: It was proposed that extra dimensions can acquire large size by higher dimensional inflation connecting two large hierarchies in particle physics and cosmology, namely the weakness of the actual gravitational force to the largeness of the observable universe, in terms of one fundamental scale. This proposal is consistent with the observed approximate scale invariant power spectrum of primordial density perturbations only for one or two extra dimensions of around the micron size. Assuming a stabilisation mechanism of the extra dimensions at the end of inflation, here we propose a cosmological history that describes the Universe evolution after the end of inflation up to the reheating temperature, that guarantees the absence of bulk gravitons at earlier times, avoiding their overproduction in the early universe. The proposed cosmological history connects the period of higher dimensional inflation to the beginning of the standard cosmology.

</details>

### [20] [Exact Solution of the Non-minimally Coupled Klein-Gordon Equation in the Schwarzschild Star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19433)
*Reynan A. Dulinayan,Kevin T. Grosvenor*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次给出了含非最小曲率标量耦合的Klein-Gordon方程在Schwarzschild恒星（均匀密度完美流体球对称恒星）背景下的精确解，解以一般Heun函数表示。通过几何诱导的代数坐标变换揭示了隐藏的Fuchs结构，在低致密极限下恢复了已知的领头阶和次领头阶结果，并在Buchdahl极限下推导了静态模的正则条件，解析描述了动态模的振幅和振荡波矢在趋近恒星中心压力奇点时的发散行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 首次获得Schwarzschild恒星背景下含非最小曲率标量耦合的Klein-Gordon方程的精确解，填补该领域精确解缺失的空白。

Method: 通过几何诱导的代数坐标变换，将问题转化为具有隐藏Fuchs结构的微分方程，解用一般Heun函数表示；在低致密极限下做渐近展开恢复已知结果；在Buchdahl极限下分析静态和动态模的行为。

Result: 得到了含非最小耦合的Klein-Gordon方程在Schwarzschild恒星背景下的精确Heun函数解；低致密极限下恢复了已知的领头阶和次领头阶结果；Buchdahl极限下得到静态模的正则条件，并发现动态模在中心压力奇点处振幅和波矢发散。

Conclusion: 该精确解为研究致密恒星背景下标量场的动力学提供了完备的理论框架，揭示了Buchdahl极限下奇点行为与Heun函数解之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We present for the first time the exact solution of the massive Klein-Gordon equation in the Schwarzschild star (perfect-fluid, uniform-density, spherically-symmetric star), including the non-minimal curvature-scalar coupling. The solution is expressed in terms of the general Heun function. A geometry-induced algebraic coordinate transformation reveals a hidden Fuchsian structure that underlies the exact solvability. Known leading- and next-to-leading-order results are recovered in the low-compactness limit. In the Buchdahl limit, we derive a regularity condition for static modes and describe analytically the divergence in amplitude and oscillation wave vector of dynamic modes as they approach the pressure singularity at the center of the star.

</details>


### [21] [Deriving effective descriptions and signal predictions for dynamical gravitational systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19435)
*Steven B. Giddings,Madhur Mehta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于腔边界作用的有效理论框架，用于描述引力系统（如双星）的辐射。通过引入围绕天体的腔体并在其边界上定义有效作用量，可以系统地推导出可观测的辐射波形和相位偏移，特别适用于研究经典黑洞行为的量子修正或其他新物理效应对引力波信号的影响。论文主要以标量辐射为例说明原理，并概述了向引力波情形的扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主要动机是建立一种系统性的方法来推断经典黑洞行为的修正（如量子力学一致性所要求的黑洞演化修正，或其他新黑洞行为模型）对引力波信号的影响。特别是，累积相位偏移被认为对旋近阶段的小的新效应具有敏感性。

Method: 基于腔边界作用（cavity action）的参数化方法：在天体周围引入腔体，在边界上定义有效作用量来描述动力学，以此替代传统的世界线有效场论方法，避免了对截断的依赖。论文以标量辐射为例展示原理，并概述了向引力波情形的扩展。

Result: 给出了黑洞以及黑洞行为修正简单模型的腔描述示例，展示了腔有效描述如何与可观测量的波形细节和累积相位偏移相联系。

Conclusion: 腔有效描述提供了一种系统性的方法来推导和参数化修正黑洞行为的辐射效应，特别是相位偏移，这对于从引力波信号中探测微小的新物理效应具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate top-down derivations of effective descriptions for radiation from gravitational systems such as binaries. With a specified cutoff prescription, one can derive worldline effective field theories, but the cutoff dependence also complicates their description. We investigate a related effective approach, based on parameterizing dynamics in terms of an action on the boundaries of cavities encompassing individual bodies. We give examples of such cavity descriptions for black holes and for simple models for modifications of their behavior. We also show how cavity effective descriptions connect to observable quantities -- detailed wave profiles, and importantly, accumulated phase shift of emitted signals. A primary motivation is to have a systematic approach to inferring effects of modification of classical black hole behavior, such as those motivated by the need for black hole evolution to be consistent with quantum mechanics, or by other models for new BH behavior, on gravitational wave signals; the latter phase shifts have in particular been argued to provide sensitivity to small new effects from the inspiral phase. To illustrate basic principles and methods, this paper largely focuses on examples with scalar radiation, but we outline extension of the analysis to gravitational wave contexts.

</details>


### [22] [Dynamical Tidal Response of Neutron Stars: from Effective Field Theory to Gravitational Waveforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19446)
*Thomas Apostolidis,Valerio De Luca,Leonardo Gualtieri,Takuya Katagiri,Paolo Pani,Luca Santoni*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了中子星在全相对论框架下到频率二阶的动力学潮汐响应，通过世界线有效场论与相对论恒星模型微扰理论结合，首次完整推导了致密双星系统动力学潮汐修正对保守动力学和引力波信号的贡献，发现动力学效应不能仅由模式激发完全描述，且动力学Love数在相对较小致密度下显著增强，对晚期旋近阶段产生不可忽略的影响，第三代探测器有望对其进行测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波模型对中子星潮汐效应的处理主要基于静态或绝热近似，而实际双星旋近过程中潮汐场是随时间变化的，动力学潮汐效应尚未被完整且系统地纳入相对论框架，可能导致对静态Love数及核物质状态方程的推断产生偏差。

Method: 结合世界线有效场论（EFT）与相对论恒星模型微扰理论，采用维度正则化方法，通过一致性匹配程序推导了外部时变场诱导的潮汐形变（含对数跑动项），并利用Fisher矩阵分析评估了第三代探测器对动力学Love数的可测量性。

Result: 首次得到完整的领头阶动力学潮汐修正（含守恒动力学和引力波相位）；发现动力学效应不能完全由模式激发描述，存在依赖于恒星致密度、物态方程和跑动项的额外贡献；动力学Love数在较小致密度下显著增强；动力学潮汐效应在8阶后牛顿阶进入引力波相位，但在晚期旋近阶段贡献不可忽略；第三代探测器可测量多种质量和物态方程下的动力学Love数；忽略该效应会导致静态Love数推断的显著偏差。

Conclusion: 动力学潮汐效应对未来高精度引力波建模至关重要，必须纳入考虑以避免对核物态方程的推断偏差，第三代探测器有望实现对其的观测约束。

Abstract: We investigate the fully relativistic dynamical tidal response of neutron stars up to second order in the frequency. Combining the worldline effective field theory for extended gravitating bodies with perturbation theory of relativistic stellar models, we derive the tidal deformation induced by an external time-dependent field, including a universal logarithmic running term. In the effective theory, we work in dimensional regularization and, through a consistent matching procedure, obtain for the first time the complete leading-order dynamical tidal corrections to both the conservative dynamics and the gravitational-wave signal of compact binaries, including the scheme-dependent finite terms in addition to the running. We show that, in the relativistic regime, dynamical effects cannot be fully captured by mode excitations alone. The magnitude of the additional contribution depends on the stellar compactness, the equation of state, and the running term. Dynamical Love numbers are significantly enhanced with respect to their static counterparts for relatively small compactness. As a result, although they formally enter the gravitational-wave phase at 8th post-Newtonian order, dynamical tidal effects yield a non-negligible contribution during the late inspiral. Using a Fisher-matrix analysis, we show that third-generation detectors such as the Einstein Telescope could measure dynamical Love numbers for a range of neutron-star masses and equations of state. Conversely, neglecting these effects can lead to significant biases in the inference of static Love numbers, and hence on the nuclear equation of state. Our results highlight the importance of dynamical tidal effects for high-precision gravitational-wave modeling with future detectors.

</details>


### [23] [Exact vacuum FLRW solutions in $q$-deformed Brans-Dicke cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19563)
*Salih Kibaroğlu,Mustafa Senay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在空间平坦的FLRW时空中研究了Brans-Dicke引力的q-变形扩展，通过修改引力强度的耦合函数引入形变，得到了广义Friedmann方程。在无物质情形下，获得了尺度因子和Brans-Dicke标量场的精确解析解，并将标量贡献重构为有效流体。标量对应的状态方程参数和减速参数均为常数，仅依赖于Brans-Dicke耦合参数ω和变形函数，使得标量扇区能够在参数空间的受限区域中模拟辐射、物质或暗能量行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索q-变形对Brans-Dicke引力的影响，研究变形耦合函数如何改变有效引力强度，并分析标量场在宇宙演化中的角色。

Method: 在空间平坦FLRW度规下，引入q-变形耦合函数修改Brans-Dicke引力的作用量，推导广义Friedmann方程；在无物质情形下求解尺度因子和标量场的精确解析解；将标量场贡献重新表述为有效理想流体，并计算其状态方程参数和减速参数。

Result: 得到了尺度因子和Brans-Dicke标量场的精确解析解；标量扇区的状态方程参数和减速参数均为常数，仅由ω和变形函数决定；在参数空间的特定区域内，标量扇区可分别模拟辐射（w=1/3）、物质（w=0）或暗能量（w<-1/3）行为。

Conclusion: q-变形Brans-Dicke引力中的标量扇区能够统一描述辐射、物质和暗能量阶段的宇宙演化，且其动力学完全由两个参数（ω和变形函数）控制，为构建统一宇宙学模型提供了新途径。

Abstract: We study a $q$-deformed extension of Brans-Dicke gravity in a spatially flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker space-time. The deformation enters through a coupling function that modifies the effective gravitational strength and leads to generalized Friedmann equations. In the matter-free sector, we obtain exact analytic solutions for the scale factor and the Brans-Dicke scalar field, and recast the scalar contribution as an effective fluid. We show that the corresponding equation-of-state parameter and the deceleration parameter are constants and depend only on the Brans-Dicke coupling $ω$ and the deformation function, allowing the scalar sector to mimic radiation-, matter-, or dark-energy-like behavior for a restricted region of parameter space.

Abstract: It has been observed that the Universe is permeated by the cosmic photon background, ranging from radio waves to gamma rays. We find that the resulting graviton background is dominated by the contribution generated in blazar jets. Importantly, this graviton background constitutes a graviton floor for high-frequency gravitational wave detectors searching for new physics, analogous to the neutrino floor.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

  Using the geometrical optics approximation, we derive the effective metric governing photon propagation and study the resulting shifts in the photon sphere. Based on this modified propagation, we compute the quasinormal modes in the eikonal limit and examine their dependence on the polarization modes. We further analyze gravitational lensing observables, focusing on the deflection angle, incorporating the polarization-dependent corrections.

### [26] [Photon surfaces extension in general spherical dust collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19809)
*Roberto Giambò,Camilla Lucamarini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将光子球面分析从零能量函数（边缘束缚）情形推广到一般非零能量函数的Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi（LTB）塌缩模型，证明了外部光子球面r=3M向内部塌缩尘埃云的唯一物理扩展是出射径向零测地线生成的零超曲面，并建立了光子球面到达中心奇点当且仅当奇点裸露的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将先前在边缘束缚（k(x)=0）LTB模型中发展的光子球面动力学系统分析推广到一般非边缘束缚情形，以检验该框架的普适性。

Method: 推导k(x)≠0情形下的LTB度规光子球面方程，将其转化为非自治一阶动力学系统；利用隐式解与常微分方程比较定理进行定性分析。

Result: 外部光子球面r=3M向塌缩尘埃云内部的唯一物理延拓是出射径向零测地线生成的零超曲面；光子球面到达中心奇点当且仅当奇点裸露。

Conclusion: 将边缘束缚情形的结论成功推广至一般LTB模型，揭示了裸奇点与黑洞（被覆盖奇点）端态之间的结构二分性，并讨论了其在黑洞阴影早期演化中可能的观测特征。

Abstract: We extend the analysis of photon surfaces in spherical dust collapse to the general, non-marginally bound case, i.e.\ allowing the \textit{energy function} $k(x)$ of the Lemaître--Tolman--Bondi (LTB) model to be non-zero. Starting from the dynamical-systems formulation developed in our previous work for the marginally bound case (arXiv:2509.01368), we derive the photon surface equations for the LTB metric with $k(x)\neq 0$, and we recast the geometric condition for a timelike hypersurface to be a photon surface as a non-autonomous first-order dynamical system. Even though the LTB evolution equation does not integrate in closed form when $k(x)\neq 0$, the implicit solutions available in the literature, together with comparison theorems for ordinary differential equations, are sufficient to show that the only physically acceptable extension of the exterior photon sphere $r=3M$ into the collapsing dust cloud is a null hypersurface, generated by outgoing radial null geodesics. Combining this fact with the known results on the causal structure of the general LTB model, we then establish that the photon surface reaches the central singularity if and only if the singularity is naked, thereby extending to the general case the picture already known in the marginally bound regime. The structural dichotomy between the naked and covered end states is also discussed in connection with possible observational signatures in the early-time evolution of black-hole shadows.

### [27] [Covariant Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations in Energy-Momentum Squared Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19879)
*Eduardo Bittencourt,Mariam Campbell,Peter K. S. Dunsby,Sergio E. Jorás*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在能量-动量平方引力框架下，利用协变1+1+2半正交形式体系研究了静态球对称恒星结构，证明非线性物质修正可重新解释为有效完美流体，使恒星平衡方程保持TOV形式，并通过平面动力系统给出了恒星相空间的全局定性描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展广义相对论框架，研究非线性物质修正对恒星结构的影响，特别是在能量-动量平方引力中理解静态球对称恒星配置的整体定性行为。

Method: 采用协变1+1+2半正交形式体系，将非线性物质修正重新解释为有效完美流体，建立以有效变量表示的恒星平衡方程；利用平面动力系统分析有限和渐近临界点，给出恒星相空间的全局定性描述。

Result: (1) 非线性物质修正可视为有效完美流体，平衡方程保持TOV形式；(2) 存在有效闭合关系时，方程可约化为自治平面动力系统；(3) 线性物态方程下可恢复GR基准，识别出精确、渐近或分段等价于GR的扇区；(4) 尘埃构型中平面约化失效，需考虑三维协变流；(5) 外时空保持Schwarzschild，表面匹配条件为p_eff(R)=0，不一定与p(R)=0重合。

Conclusion: 能量-动量平方引力中的恒星结构可通过有效变量与GR形式对应，其相空间结构更丰富，且对于自束缚物质，恒星表面的物理压强和有效压强零点可能不同。

Abstract: We study static, spherically symmetric stellar configurations in an extended class of Energy--Momentum Squared Gravity using the covariant \(1+1+2\) semi-tetrad formalism. For perfect physical fluids, we show that the nonlinear matter corrections can be reinterpreted as an effective perfect fluid, so that the stellar equilibrium equations retain the standard Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff form when written in terms of effective variables. The resulting covariant structure equations are formulated in both metric and dimensionless variables and, whenever an effective closure relation exists, reduce to an autonomous planar dynamical system. This provides a global qualitative description of the stellar phase space in terms of finite and asymptotic critical points.
  Specializing to linear physical equations of state, we recover the general relativistic benchmark and identify sectors that are exactly, asymptotically, or piecewise equivalent to general relativity, as well as sectors -- particularly dust configurations -- for which the planar reduction breaks down and the full three-dimensional covariant flow must be considered. We further recover the standard metric Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff equation in terms of effective variables and show that, although the exterior spacetime remains Schwarzschild, the natural matching condition at the stellar surface is \(p_{\rm eff}(R)=0\), which need not coincide with \(p(R)=0\) for self-bound matter.

</details>


### [28] [Cosmological Constraints on Minimal Cubic Galileon Models in Teleparallel Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19905)
*Akbar Davlataliev,Abdurakhmon Nosirov,Odil Yunusov,Bobomurat Ahmedov,Jackson Levi Said*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越标准ΛCDM范式，探索teleparallel引力框架下三次Galileon模型解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀的观测可行性。

Method: 采用teleparallel引力框架，引入偏离标准TEGR的模型参数b1，考虑二次势与指数势两种标量场势，构建四种场景（自由b1与固定b1=2）。使用Pantheon+ Ia型超新星样本、宇宙时钟测量、SH0ES信息及BAO数据对模型参数进行观测约束。

Result: 固定b1=2的二次势模型在包含BAO数据时χ²_min低于ΛCDM，AIC准则下支持度相当；但BIC准则仍偏好ΛCDM。不同势函数和b1固定与否的选择影响统计偏好。

Abstract: Cubic Galileon cosmological models provide a well-motivated framework for investigating late-time cosmic acceleration beyond the standard $Λ$CDM paradigm. In this work, we study observational constraints on cubic Galileon models within the teleparallel gravity framework, where deviations from the standard teleparallel equivalent of general relativity are encoded through the model parameter $b_1$. We consider two scalar-field potentials, namely quadratic and exponential potentials, and analyze four representative scenarios: quadratic and exponential potentials with $b_1$ treated as a free parameter, together with the corresponding cases in which $b_1=2$ is fixed. Using the $\text{Pantheon}^+$ Type Ia supernova sample, cosmic chronometer measurements, SH0ES information, and baryon acoustic oscillation data, we constrain the cosmological and model parameters and compare the observational viability of the different scenarios. We find that the considered teleparallel cubic Galileon models can accommodate the late-time expansion history, although the statistical preference depends on the choice of potential and on whether $b_1$ is fixed or varied. In particular, the fixed-$b_1$ model with a quadratic potential provides the most competitive fit among the Galileon scenarios when BAO data are included, showing a lower $χ^2_{\min}$ than $Λ$CDM and comparable support according to the AIC criterion. However, the BIC criterion continues to favor the minimal $Λ$CDM model because of the larger parameter space of the extended models. These results suggest that teleparallel cubic Galileon cosmologies remain phenomenologically viable, while a stronger claim regarding the Hubble tension requires further consistency tests.

### [29] [On the Plebanski Formulation with Energy Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20042)
*Jack C. M. Hughes,Joudy F. Jamal Beek,Fedor V. Kusmartsev*

TL;DR: 本文系统构建了Plebanski引力理论中物质源的显式表达式，通过Kulkarni-Nomizu积将无迹能量-动量张量提升为代数曲率的(1,1)分量并提取手征成分，证明了手征场方程与守恒律的一致性，并以Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter解为例验证了该构造的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Plebanski形式中物质耦合不如度规形式直接，因为能量-动量张量是对称的，而Plebanski变量自然取值于2-形式的自对偶/反自对偶Hodge分解中，需要建立系统的映射方案。

Method: 通过Kulkarni-Nomizu积将无迹能量-动量张量提升到代数曲率空间的(1,1)分量，再提取其手征分量得到Plebanski物质源T^i，并与Krasnov基于自对偶基的定义进行验证。

Result: 该构造复现了Krasnov的定义；验证了物质耦合手征场方程通过手征Bianchi恒等式d^A F^i=0导出通常的守恒律∇_μT^{μν}=0；应用于球对称电磁应力-能量张量得到Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter解。

Conclusion: 提供了一套将度规物质源系统翻译为Plebanski场方程所需反自对偶源项的系统化处方。

Abstract: In Plebanski's formulation the coupling of matter is less direct than in the metric formulation since the energy-momentum tensor $T_{μν}$ is symmetric, while the Plebanski variables are naturally valued in the self-dual/anti-self-dual Hodge decomposition of 2-forms. An explicit construction of the Plebanski matter source $T^i$ is obtained by lifting the trace-free energy-momentum tensor $\hat T_{μν}$ into the $(1,1)$ component of the algebraic curvature space using the Kulkarni-Nomizu product, and then extracting its chiral components. This construction reproduces the definition for $T^i$ in terms of the self-dual basis $Σ^i$ and $\hat T_{μν}$ introduced by Krasnov. We also verify that the matter-coupled chiral field equations imply the usual conservation law $\nabla_μT^{μν}=0$ through the chiral Bianchi identity $d^A F^i=0$. As an application, the construction is applied to a spherically symmetric electromagnetic stress-energy tensor, where the anti-self-dual part of the matter-coupled Plebanski field equations yields the Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter solution. The result gives a systematic prescription for translating metric matter sources into the anti-self-dual source terms required by the Plebanski field equations.

### [30] [Regular Black Holes from Anisotropic Source with Hydrodynamic Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20109)
*Hassan Firouzjahi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究各向异性能动张量源下的正则黑洞解，通过引入流体力学状态方程P=P(ρ)推导出多种正则黑洞度量，发现声速平方在P取极大值处变号导致流体力学不稳定性，且亚光速约束排除了能量密度指数衰减的模型，并建立了强能量条件破坏点、P零点与P极大点之间的普适层级关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由各向异性能动张量源驱动的正则黑洞解，理解其内部几何结构趋近dS度规的机制，并分析状态方程P(ρ)的不同形式对黑洞解的影响。

Method: 将能动张量分解为各向同性和各向异性分量，假设流体力学状态方程P=P(ρ)，在球对称条件下求解正则黑洞解，分析声速平方c_s^2的行为及亚光速约束，研究强能量条件的违背顺序。

Result: 获得多种已知及新型正则黑洞度规；P(ρ)在大距离处存在根和极大值；c_s^2在P极大值点变号，表明流体力学不稳定性；亚光速约束排除能量密度指数衰减模型；建立了SEC破坏点、P零点与P极大点之间的普适层级关系。

Conclusion: 正则黑洞解中状态方程的行为会导致潜在流体力学不稳定性，且受到亚光速条件的严格限制，不同物理临界点之间存在普适的层级顺序。

Abstract: We study regular black hole solutions sourced by an anisotropic energy momentum tensor. It is well known that the geometry of the interior of a spherically symmetric regular black hole approaches the dS metric. Having decomposed the energy momentum tensor into its isotropic and anisotropic components, we assume a hydrodynamic equation of state, $P= P(ρ)$, for the pressure, and look for spherically symmetric, regular black hole solutions. We consider different forms of $ P(ρ)$ which yield the previously known regular black hole solutions, as well as various new metrics. We show that the profile of $ P(ρ)$ has a root and a maximum as it approaches $0^+$ at large distances. Consequently, the square of the sound speed of perturbations, $c_s^2$, changes sign at the point where $P$ reaches its maximum, indicating a potential hydrodynamic instability. In addition, imposing the subluminal bound on $c_s$ puts strong constraints on the model parameters, excluding models in which the energy density has an exponential fall off. We establish a universal hierarchy among the relative positions at which the strong energy condition is violated, at which $P$ has its root, and at which $P$ attains its maximum.

### [31] [The auxiliary-metric formulation of Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20247)
*Bayram Tekin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入辅助度规将Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity (BINMG)重新表述为多项式形式，简化了该理论的分析，并揭示了其与Einstein引力的比例关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BINMG通过度规与Einstein张量平移的行列式将New Massive Gravity推广到所有曲率阶数，但其无穷级数形式在分析上较为复杂。本文旨在通过辅助度规重新表述BINMG，使其成为多项式形式，从而简化理论分析。

Method: 引入独立辅助度规 $q_{\mu\nu}$，其代数运动方程 $q_{\mu\nu}=g_{\mu\nu} + \frac{\sigma}{m^2} G_{\mu\nu}(g)$ 精确恢复正则分支上的行列式作用量，并将无穷曲率级数求和为单一关系。通过密度化变量 $P^{\mu\nu} = \sqrt{-q}\, q^{\mu\nu}$，三维作用量变为多项式形式，所有导数依赖由耦合项 $P^{\mu\nu} G_{\mu\nu}(g)$ 承载。

Result: 新表述大幅简化了代数运算：唯一真空的推导一行即可完成；二次作用量给出单一Pauli-Fierz有质量自旋-2场，且Fierz-Pauli调谐是自然生成而非人为施加的。在局域AdS背景上，守恒荷、BTZ质量和角动量、中心荷及熵均简化为Einstein结果乘以一个公共因子。该表述还以正确变量隔离了非线性自由度问题。

Conclusion: 辅助度规表述使BINMG的理论性质以更简洁的代数方式呈现，并为后续完整的Dirac自由度计数研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity (BINMG) completes New Massive Gravity to all orders in curvature through the determinant of the metric shifted by the Einstein tensor. We recast it with an independent auxiliary metric $q_{μν}$, whose algebraic equation of motion $q_{μν}=g_{μν}+\fracσ{m^2}G_{μν}(g)$ recovers the determinant action exactly on the regular branch and resums the infinite curvature series into a single relation. In the densitized variable $P^{μν}=\sqrt{-q}\,q^{μν}$ the three-dimensional action is polynomial, with all derivative dependence carried by the coupling $P^{μν}G_{μν}(g)$. The formulation makes known properties follow with substantially less algebra: the unique vacuum follows in one line, and the quadratic action yields a single Pauli-Fierz massive spin-2 field with the Fierz-Pauli tuning generated rather than imposed. On locally AdS backgrounds the conserved charges, BTZ mass and angular momentum, central charge, and entropy reduce to the Einstein results times a common factor. The formulation also isolates the nonlinear degree-of-freedom problem in the right variables, leaving the full Dirac count to separate work.

</details>

Abstract: The Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer (WDM) time-frequency transform has been widely used in gravitational-wave astronomy, yet a self-contained, mathematically explicit reference for practitioners remains lacking. This is especially true for those wishing to adopt the transform in modern Python and JAX inference workflows. We present wdm_transform, an open-source Python package implementing the WDM wavelet-packet time-frequency transform, and document its mathematical foundations, statistical properties, and practical implementation for gravitational-wave data analysis. The package supplies NumPy and JAX backends, both transforms (forward and inverse) validated to floating-point precision, with the JAX backend enabling GPU-accelerated transforms of million-point data streams in tens of milliseconds. As a worked example, we verify that the WDM-domain likelihood reproduces frequency-domain posteriors for a resolved LISA galactic binary under a shared stationary noise model, confirming numerical equivalence of the two representations in that controlled setting. This work paves the way for systematic optimisation of WDM tilings, a particularly promising direction for the non-stationary noise, stochastic backgrounds, and data gaps anticipated in future detectors, and for direct comparisons with alternative time-frequency representations needed to meet the challenges of future gravitational-wave data analysis.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该工作建立了局部NLED响应与观测者屏幕上极化依赖的临界结构之间的直接几何联系，揭示了非线性电动力学在旋转黑洞背景下导致双折射的机制，为未来引力波天文学和高能天体物理观测提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study high-frequency electromagnetic propagation in the rotating García--Díaz solution of Einstein gravity coupled to NLED. Starting from the mixed electromagnetic potentials, we project the field $F$ and the excitation $P$ on a principal tetrad and obtain the aligned scalars $E$, $B$, $D$ and $H$. These scalars allow us to reconstruct the regular local constitutive branch connected with Maxwell theory through the map $(D,B)\mapsto(E,H)$. We then insert the resulting response matrix into the Fresnel characteristic problem. At the perturbative order considered here, the Fresnel quartic factorizes into two quadratic branches, each defining an effective optical metric. Both optical metrics admit Carter-type separation of the Hamilton--Jacobi equation and possess their own radial and angular potentials, critical constants and unstable critical families. By projecting these families onto the celestial sphere of a finite-distance observer, we obtain two critical contours, $Γ_+$ and $Γ_-$, which coincide in the Maxwell limit and split when the nonlinear constitutive response is active. We quantify this birefringent splitting through the maximum angular separation, the relative diameter shift and the normalized birefringent width. Numerical scans over the nonlinear coupling, spin and observer inclination show that the splitting is generated by the constitutive response, redistributed by rotation and stable under local projection changes within the perturbative domain. This provides a direct geometrical link between the local NLED response and a polarization-dependent critical structure on the observer screen.

Abstract: In PRL 129, 110401 it was shown that it is theoretically possible to have operationally detectable causal loops without violating the principle of no superluminal signalling (NSS) in (1+1)-Minkowski spacetime. *Apratim Ganguly,Radouane Gannouji,Akshay Kumar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了高阶Lovelock引力理论中球对称尘埃坍缩的局部宇宙监督问题，发现Lovelock项不恢复但反而促进局部宇宙监督的破坏，使得中心奇点可被外部观测者看见。非临界维度下视界形成指数β_N=(D-1)/(D-1-2N)控制奇点可见性，临界维度D=2N+1下所有向外开放的奇点曲线均导致局部可见。可见奇点沿出射零测地线为Królak强，在阈值处达到Tipler强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验在广义相对论之外的高曲率修正引力理论（Lovelock引力）中，局部宇宙监督猜想是否成立，即奇点是否会被事件视界遮蔽。

Method: 解析分析球对称尘埃坍缩在Lovelock引力中的动力学行为，研究不同维度、不同Lovelock阶数N下奇点曲线与视界曲线的标度关系，推导局部可见性条件ℓ<β_N。

Result: 非临界维度下视界捕获指数为β_N=(D-1)/(D-1-2N)，奇点可见条件为ℓ<β_N；临界奇数维度D=2N+1下无近中心视界形成，所有向外开放的奇点曲线均导致局部可见。可见奇点沿出射零测地线为Królak强，阈值处达Tipler强。

Conclusion: Lovelock高阶项不恢复局部宇宙监督，反而促进局部可见奇点的形成，且Lovelock阶数N越大，导致局部可见的非均匀初始数据类越宽。

Abstract: We show that higher-curvature Lovelock terms do not restore local cosmic censorship in spherical dust collapse, but instead promote the local visibility of central shell-focusing singularities. On the collapse branch with positive highest-order Lovelock coefficient \(c_N\), the highest nonvanishing Lovelock order \(N\) controls both the near-singularity collapse and the formation of trapped surfaces. In noncritical dimensions, \(D-1-2N>0\), the apparent-horizon curve approaches the singularity curve with trapping exponent \(β_N=(D-1)/(D-1-2N)\). Comparing this scale with the first nonvanishing correction \(r^\ell\) to the singularity curve gives the local-visibility condition \(\ell<β_N\), provided the singularity curve opens outward. Thus increasing \(N\) enlarges the class of inhomogeneous initial data producing outgoing radial null rays from the central singularity. In the critical odd-dimensional branch, \(D=2N+1\), no apparent horizon forms sufficiently close to the center, so any outward opening of the singularity curve gives local visibility. The locally visible singularities are Królak-strong along the emerging null rays, with Tipler strength reached at threshold. For bound and unbound collapse, the noncritical exponents are unchanged: the energy function modifies the opening of the singularity curve, while in the critical branch it enters the leading terminal collapse velocity.

</details>

### [37] [The Kernel of the $\hat A$-Genus in Rational Spin Bordism is Generated by Ricci-Positive Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19505)
*Gerald Höhn,Philipp Höhn*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文证明了在有理Spin配边环中，正Ricci曲率流形的配边类恰好张成$\hat A$-示性数的核。通过构造奇数次光滑完全交截Fano流形作为生成元，并利用多项式插值论证显示其生成元的线性无关性，完整地回答了复椭圆属背景下关于正Ricci曲率有理配边障碍的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复椭圆属的背景下，人们提出了关于正Ricci曲率的有理配边障碍问题，即寻找正Ricci曲率流形所代表的配边类在有理Spin配边环中的刻画特征。

Method: 构造奇数次光滑完全交截$Y_{m,\ell}\subset \mathbb{CP}^{2m+\ell}$（$\ell$为奇数），这些流形是Spin且Fano的，从而具有正Ricci曲率度量。利用$\hat A$-示性数的一阶加厚在$(J/J^2)_{4m}$上诱导$m-1$个线性泛函，其在$[Y_{m,\ell}]$上的取值由严格递增次数的多项式$P_{m,q}(\ell)$决定，通过多项式插值论证证明满秩性。

Result: 在每个维度上，正Ricci曲率Spin流形的配边类在有理意义下恰好张成$\hat A$-示性数的核$J=\ker(\hat A:R\to\mathbb{Q}[u])$，即$J$中每个元都可表示为正Ricci曲率流形的有理线性组合。

Conclusion: 完整回答了复椭圆属背景下关于正Ricci曲率有理配边障碍的问题，在可微有理Spin范畴中给出了正Ricci曲率的精确配边刻画。

Abstract: We prove that, in every degree, the rational Spin bordism classes represented by manifolds admitting metrics with positive Ricci curvature span exactly the kernel of the $\hat A$-genus. More precisely, for \[ R=Ω_*^{Spin}\otimes\mathbb{Q},\qquad J=\ker(\hat A:R\longrightarrow\mathbb{Q}[u]),\] the $\mathbb{Q}$-span of bordism classes of Ricci-positive Spin manifolds equals $J$ in each degree. This answers, in the differentiable rational Spin category, a question about rational bordism obstructions to positive Ricci curvature which was raised in the context of complex elliptic genera.
  The proof uses smooth complete intersections of an odd number $\ell$ of quadrics \[ Y_{m,\ell}\subset \mathbb{CP}^{2m+\ell}, \qquad \ell=1,\, 3,\, \ldots,\, 2m-1. \] These manifolds have real dimension $4m$, are Spin and Fano, and therefore admit metrics with positive Ricci curvature. A first-order thickening of the $\hat A$-genus induces $m-1$ linear functionals on $(J/J^2)_{4m}$. Their values on the classes $[Y_{m,\ell}]$ are governed by polynomials $P_{m,q}(\ell)$ of strictly increasing degrees $q+1=1$, $2$, $\ldots$, $m-1$. This gives full rank by a polynomial-interpolation argument.

Result: 证明了当(V,M)满足可粘合条件时，Z的卷积代数同构于两个nil-Hecke代数的交；建立了该代数的极点和留数描述；将结果推广到环群情形。

Abstract: Given a complex reductive group $G$, a representation $V$ of $G$ and a Borel-stable subspace $M \subset V$, we consider the associated Steinberg-type variety $Z$. We also provide a description of these new algebras in terms of poles and residues. Similar results are obtained when $G$ is replaced by its loop group. This generalizes results of Ginzburg, Kapranov and Vasserot describing the affine Hecke algebra and DAHA, as well as a result of Teleman and Gannon--Webster that realizes certain Coulomb branches by gluing two copies of the universal centralizer.

Abstract: We prove several results about Stiefel-Whitney Classes (SWCs) $w_k(π)$ of representations $π$ of $S_n$. First, each SWC is polynomial in the character values of $π$ at involutions. Next, for a fixed $k$, the proportion of irreducible $π$ for which $w_k(π)=0$ approaches $100\%$ as $n \to \infty$. A similar result holds for the top SWCs. We also provide a simple criterion which determines the first nonvanishing SWC for a representation. The first four SWCs are computed explicitly. Finally, we give analogues for alternating groups.

### [43] [Characters of modules over negative rank-2 Borcherds-Kac-Moody Lie algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20386)
*Souvik Pal,Supravat Sarkar,G. Krishna Teja*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究Borcherds-Kac-Moody Lie代数中，对应于新型符号支配积分锥P^±中权μ的非可积最高权模L(μ)的结构。在秩2情形下，研究了Verma覆盖M(μ)中的模结构和极大向量，探讨了Kac-Kazhdan关于线性无关极大向量计数下界的严格性，并在Kac-Kazhdan方程在根锥内部有唯一解时给出了所有V的表示和特征标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在秩2情形下，通过分析Verma覆盖M(μ)的权空间，研究Kac-Kazhdan关于线性无关极大向量计数下界的严格性（是否一致取等）。利用Kac-Kazhdan方程在根锥内部有唯一解的条件，推导所有模V的表示和特征标。

Abstract: Let $\mathfrak{g}=\mathfrak{g}(A)$ be the Borcherds-Kac-Moody Lie algebra (BKM LA), corresponding to a BKM Cartan matrix $A$ filled by negative integers. Let $P^+\subset \mathfrak{h}^*$ the classical dominant integral cone (wherein pairings are non-negative). The non-integrable simple highest weight modules $L(μ)$'s widely studied were broadly those by Naito ([Trans. Amer. Soc., 1995]), for $μ$'s dot-linked to $P^+$-translates of sums $- \sum_{j\in J}α_j$ of mutually orthogonal and imaginary simple roots $α_j$'s.
  Recently, we computed weights of all highest weight $\mathfrak{g}$-modules $V$'s, and characters of $L(ρ)$ for Weyl vector $ρ$ in negative type-$A$. These needed a family of ``integrable'' $L(μ)$'s for $μ$'s inside our novel signed-dominant-integral cone $P^{\pm}$ (which generalizes $P^+$). Pairings $μ(α_i^{\vee})\leq 0$ therein are multiples of $\frac{A_{ii}}{2}$ for all $i$. Nevertheless, $L(μ)$ contain ``Chevalley-Serre relations'' $f_i^{\frac{2}{A_{ii}}{μ(α_i^{\vee})}+1}L(μ)_μ=0$; which differ from relations in $L(λ)$ for all $λ\in P^+$, and are seemingly unstudied earlier (also by Naito).
  This paper initiates the study in rank-2, of the module structures and maximal vectors (or Verma embeddings) in the Verma covers $M(μ)$ of $L(μ)$'s for $μ\in P^{\pm}$. In this, our goal is to explore in weight spaces of those Verma covers, the strictness (or otherwise, an uniform equality) of lower bounds by Kac and Kazhdan ([Adv. Math., 1979]) for count of linearly independent maximal vectors. We obtain presentations and characters of all $V$'s when Kac-Kazhdan equation has unique solution in the interior of root-cone. This builds on the unique solution case in Lemma 3.1 from that paper.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Torsion pairs, and in particular t-structures, play a central role in the study of triangulated categories. Specifically, t-structures induced by silting (or tilting) objects often admit desirable properties with strong connections to derived equivalences. In this paper, using the correspondence of Saorín-Šťovíček between cohereditary cotorsion pairs in Frobenius exact categories and t-structures in their stable categories, we construct a family of t-structures in the $Q$-shaped derived category of Holm and Jorgensen, arising from admissible partitions of $Q$. We give an explicit description of the associated cotorsion pairs inside the Frobenius exact category of the bifibrant objects, and we identify the corresponding co-aisles by certain homological vanishing conditions. Such t-structures are proved to be induced by a silting object, that can be completely determined by the combinatorics of $Q$. Finally, we illustrate our results by recovering well-known equivalences in the $Q$-shaped setting, while also providing examples where the combinatorial conditions fail (e.g. cyclic quivers), showing that such categories may admit no non-trivial t-structures, revealing phenomena analogous to those observed by Linckelmann in stable module categories.

Motivation: 理解非有理$C_2$-有限顶点算子代数在环面上的单点函数空间结构，特别是验证Gainutdinov-Runkel猜想，该猜想已由Gui和Zhang用不同方法建立，作者希望提供一种基于Arike-Nagatomo伪迹的互补表示论方法。

Method: 将单点函数空间与表示范畴中射影对象的子范畴的迹对象相联系；识别迹空间的对偶与射影生成子$E$的自同态代数上的对称函数；使用Arike-Nagatomo伪迹技术；在分离共形权模$\mathbb{Z}$的额外假设下，应用受Huang启发的射影覆盖技巧证明单射性。

Result: 证明了从$E$上对称函数到单点函数的Gainutdinov-Runkel映射的满射性；在分离共形权模$\mathbb{Z}$的额外假设下，还证明了该映射的单射性。

Conclusion: 本文为Gainutdinov-Runkel猜想提供了基于伪迹和射影覆盖的表示论证明，补充了Gui和Zhang的分析方法，深化了对非有理顶点算子代数环面单点函数空间的理解。

Abstract: We study the space of one-point functions on the torus for a possibly nonrational $C_2$-cofinite vertex operator algebra $V$ by relating it to a trace object of the subcategory of projective objects in the representation category of $V$. We identify the dual of the trace space with symmetric functions on the endomorphism algebra $E$ of a projective generator. Motivated by the Gainutdinov-Runkel conjecture, recently established using different methods by Gui and Zhang, we present a complementary representation-theoretic approach based on Arike-Nagatomo pseudo-traces. In this framework, we prove surjectivity of the Gainutdinov-Runkel map from symmetric functions on $E$ to one-point functions. Under the additional assumption of separated conformal weights modulo $\mathbb{Z}$, we also prove injectivity, using projective-cover techniques inspired by Huang.

</details>

### [47] [Geometric realization of affine bases: the Kronecker quiver case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19708)
*Yumeng Wu,Jie Xiao*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文从几何角度研究Kronecker箭图量子包络代数负部分中PBW基与典范基之间的转移矩阵。利用Lusztig的典范基几何构造，通过表示变体簇分层X(α,m)上的旗层复形构造了PBW基元素的层复形实现。首先给出这些旗层复形限制到分层上的单分支的几何描述，从而比较PBW型层复形与Lusztig构造中的单纯反常层IC(X(α),L_χ)，并利用相关F_q结构的纯性结果给出Lusztig反常层构成复合代数基的另一种证明。其次，将PBW基与典范基之间的转移系数几何显式化，证明这些系数由交同上同调复形限制到小子簇时局部系统的重数控制，进而得到从典范基到PBW基的转移矩阵是上三角的且对角元为1，系数具有直接几何解释。在Kronecker箭图情形下恢复了转移矩阵的三角性并得到对应系数多项式的正性性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立PBW基与典范基之间转移矩阵的几何理解，特别是通过表示簇几何和反常层理论给出转移系数的显式刻画，以深化对量子群典范基结构和PBW基关系的认识。

Method: 利用Lusztig的几何构造方法，引入旗层复形(flag sheaf complexes)实现PBW基元素；通过分析这些复形限制到不同分层上的单分支结构，并与Lusztig定义的交同上同调复形(单纯反常层)进行比较；利用有限域F_q结构的纯性结果证明基性质；通过交同上同调复形限制中局部系统的重数给出转移系数的几何解释。

Result: (1) 给出了PBW型层复形到分层X(α,m)上限制中单分支的几何描述；(2) 获得了Lusztig反常层构成复合代数基的另一种证明；(3) 证明了从典范基到PBW基的转移矩阵是上三角的，对角元为1；(4) 转移系数具有直接的几何解释，由交同上同调复形在小子簇上限制中局部系统的重数给出；(5) 在Kronecker箭图情形下恢复了转移矩阵的三角性并得到系数多项式的正性性质。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了Kronecker箭图量子包络代数中PBW基与典范基之间转移矩阵的完整几何框架，揭示了转移系数由交同上同调复形限制中局部系统重数控制的几何本质，并得到了三角性和正性等关键性质，为更一般箭图情形下的类似研究提供了方法论基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the transition matrix between the PBW basis and the canonical basis for the negative part of the quantized enveloping algebra of the Kronecker quiver from a geometric viewpoint. Building on Lusztig's geometric construction of the canonical basis, we construct sheaf-complex realizations of PBW basis elements by means of flag sheaf complexes over the strata $X(α,m)$ of representation varieties. Our first goal is to give a geometric description of the simple constituents appearing in the restrictions of these flag sheaf complexes to the strata $X(α,m)$. This allows us to compare the PBW-type sheaf complexes with the simple perverse sheaves $IC(X(α),L_χ)$ arising in Lusztig's construction. Using this description together with a purity result for the relevant $\mathbb{F}_q$-structures, we obtain another proof that the elements defined by Lusztig's perverse sheaves indeed form a basis of the composition algebra.Our second goal is to make the transition coefficients between the PBW basis and the canonical basis geometrically explicit. More precisely, we show that these coefficients are governed by the multiplicities of local systems in the restrictions of intersection cohomology complexes to smaller strata. As a consequence, the transition matrix from the canonical basis to the PBW basis is upper triangular with diagonal entries equal to $1$, and its coefficients admit a direct geometric interpretation. In particular, in the Kronecker quiver case we recover the triangularity of the transition matrix and obtain positivity properties of the corresponding coefficient polynomials.

Abstract: The construction of relations among relations is one ingredient in the Groebner-like basis construction of the maximal ideal of the universal vertex operator algebra $V^k_{\mathfrak g}$ for affine Lie algebras. For affine Lie algebras of type $C_n^{(1)}$, such combinatorially parametrized relations among relations were constructed in earlier work for level $2$ standard modules \cite{PS3}, and for $C_2^{(1)}$-standard modules at higher levels \cite{S}. This article presents two further examples in which the same counting method can be carried out. The first treats $C_n^{(1)}$-standard modules at the fixed level $k=5$, with $n$ arbitrary. The second treats $C_3^{(1)}$-standard modules for arbitrary level $k$. In both cases the calculation compares the number of required relations among relations in a trapezoid of the array of negative root vectors with the corresponding representation-theoretic dimension.

Abstract: Let $G = \mathbf{GL}_d(\mathbb{F})$ be the general linear group over a field of cardinal $q$, and let $\mathbb{k}$ be a field of positive characteristic which does not divide $q(q-1)$. The main novelty is our ability to compute these Ext-groups in higher degree than what was done before. More precisely, let $\ell$ be the order of $q$ in $\mathbb{k}$. In previous work, this method enabled the computation of the cohomology groups $H^*(\mathbf{GL}_d,M)$ in degree $*\leq \ell-1$. We show that for a lot of modules $M$, we can compute these cohomology groups in higher degree, with an example where we can compute until degree $3(\ell-1)$. We also show some new result on Ext-groups between modules over the quantum Schur algebra along the way.

### [50] [Solving Nonequilibrium Dynamics via Influence Matrix Bootstrap: Floquet-PXP Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19430)
*Xiao-Yang Yang,He-Ran Wang,Zhong Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用张量网络中的影响矩阵方法，研究了"Rule 201"量子胞自动机（PXP哈密顿量的可积Trotter化）的非平衡可积动力学。通过发展广义拉链条件（精确求解局域动力学）和数值自举方法（求解有限键维影响矩阵），揭示了初态依赖的非平衡行为，包括持续振荡在非可积微扰下的衰变、守恒律约束的非热弛豫、以及纠缠熵增长。从信息论角度，发现了多时间关联的隐马尔可夫序结构，并给出了影响矩阵的精确分裂指标矩阵乘积态表示。该框架统一描述了非热化与热化动力学，可在Rydberg原子阵列等量子模拟器中实验检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可积系统非平衡动力学的精确表征是一个重大挑战：虽然平衡态性质（基态、热力学）可高效刻画，但非平衡可积动力学缺乏统一的理论工具。现有方法难以同时处理可积精确解和非可积微扰下的热化行为。

Method: 基于影响矩阵（influence matrix）的张量网络方法，发展了两类技术：(1) 广义拉链条件（generalized zipper conditions），用于精确求解局域动力学；(2) 数值自举方法（numerical bootstrap），用于求解有限但较大键维的影响矩阵。同时引入分裂指标矩阵乘积态表示以揭示隐马尔可夫序结构。

Result: 发现了丰富的初态依赖的非平衡行为景观：获得持续振荡在局域非可积微扰下衰变的解析结果；揭示了守恒律约束的非热弛豫；数值精确计算了多种初态的纠缠熵增长；识别了多时间关联的隐马尔可夫序——动力学记忆分离为有限长度和长程分布成分。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个在同一可解模型中统一研究非热化和热化非平衡动力学的分析框架，且结果可直接在Rydberg原子阵列等量子模拟器中实验验证，为理解可积系统的非平衡动力学开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Studies of integrable systems have profoundly deepened the fundamental understanding of quantum many-body physics. While equilibrium properties such as ground states and thermodynamics can often be characterized efficiently, accurately characterizing nonequilibrium integrable dynamics remains a significant challenge. Here, we address this problem in the "Rule 201" quantum cellular automaton, an integrable Trotterization of the PXP Hamiltonian. Using the tensor-network approach of the influence matrix, we develop local conditions called generalized zipper conditions that allow exact solutions of local dynamics. We also introduce a numerical bootstrap method for solving influence matrices with finite but relatively large bond dimensions. This uncovers a rich landscape of nonequilibrium behavior exhibiting initial-state dependence. As an example, we investigate the fate of persistent oscillating dynamics under local non-integrable perturbations, and present analytical results for non-thermal relaxation constrained by conservation laws. We also obtain numerically exact results for entanglement growth across a broad class of initial states. Furthermore, from an information-theoretic perspective, we identify a refined structure of multitime correlations termed the hidden Markov order: the memory encoded in the dynamics separates into finite-length and long-range distributed components, which becomes transparent in an exact split-index matrix-product-state representation of the influence matrix. Our approach enables unified investigations of nonthermalizing and thermalizing regimes of nonequilibrium dynamics within a single analytically tractable model, and can be tested experimentally in state-of-the-art quantum simulators such as Rydberg atom arrays.

### [51] [Quantum circuit decomposition of the tangent-fermion Dirac operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19020)
*C. W. J. Beenakker*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出正切费米子离散化方法，通过将狄拉克方程写为广义本征值问题，利用局部算子束（operator pencil）在量子计算中实现高效的块编码，避免了费米子加倍问题，且LCU项数和归一化因子与晶格尺寸无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶格上的狄拉克算子无法同时满足局域性和无费米子加倍的要求，而现有的非局域、保对称性离散化在量子计算中会导致线性组合酉算子（LCU）的项数和归一化因子随晶格尺寸增长，损害量子算法的效率。

Method: 将狄拉克方程重新表述为广义本征值问题，引入局部算子束（operator pencil），其中每个算子成员具有精确的LCU表示，且项数与晶格尺寸无关，子归一化因子为常数阶（与椭圆算子相当）。

Result: 正切费米子离散化避开了费米子加倍与局域性之间的基本障碍，实现了无需费米子加倍的高效狄拉克谱和格林函数的块编码。

Conclusion: 该工作为量子计算中无费米子加倍的狄拉克算子模拟提供了高效可行的块编码原语，在量子模拟中有重要应用前景。

Abstract: The Dirac operator on a lattice cannot be both local and free of fermion doubling, at least not without breaking fundamental symmetries. Non-local, symmetry-preserving discretizations that avoid doubling have a quantum circuit representation as a linear-combination-of-unitaries (LCU) in which both the number of terms and their norm (the subnormalization factor) grow with the lattice size, compromising the efficiency of a quantum algorithm. We show that the tangent-fermion discretization escapes this obstruction when the Dirac equation is written as a generalized eigenvalue problem with a local operator pencil: Each member of the pencil has an exact LCU, with term count that is independent of lattice size and with subnormalization factor of order unity, on a par with elliptic operators. This provides an efficient block-encoding primitive for Dirac spectra and Green functions without fermion doubling.

</details>


### [52] [Indefinite Quantum Causality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19438)
*Fabio Costa,Giulia Rubino,Cyril Branciard,Časlav Brukner,Marco Túlio Quintino*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子理论中因果律的作用、量子理论与广义相对论的相互作用，以及高阶量子计算，同时挖掘不定因果序作为量子信息处理资源的潜力。

Method: 采用过程矩阵形式体系（process matrix formalism），将物理过程视为操作序列，但允许放宽因果顺序的假设，引入量子因果不定性。

Result: 不定因果序已成为量子信息处理的可行资源；综述整理了该领域的关键理论成果与实验实现。

Conclusion: 量子因果不定性是一个活跃的研究方向，兼具基础物理意义和应用价值，未来有望在量子计算与量子引力等领域发挥更大作用。

Abstract: In recent years, operational approaches to quantum foundations have been developed as a means of understanding the core principles and distinctive features of quantum theory. Such approaches typically view physical processes as sequences of operations, with earlier operations serving as causes of later effects. However, a growing literature is emerging on the possibility of relaxing this assumption and allowing for quantum indefiniteness in the causal order. This development stems from a variety of motivations, both fundamental and applied, including exploring the role of causality in quantum theory, the interplay between quantum theory and general relativity, and higher-order quantum computing. A prominent offshoot of this development is the emergence of indefinite causal order as a feasible resource for quantum information processing. This review provides an overview of the current state of the art in the field, covering the methodology underlying indefinite quantum causality within the so-called "process matrix formalism", outlining key results and experimental implementations, and discussing recent advances.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机重置已被证明是驱动量子多体系统到非平衡稳态的通用协议，但尚缺乏量子硬件层面的实验验证。

Method: 构建了含噪声的离散时间理论框架，其中幺正门与含噪声的中电路测量和条件重置交替进行；在超导量子处理器上对最多7个量子比特进行实验演示。

Abstract: Stochastic resetting has emerged as a versatile protocol to drive quantum many-body systems to non-equilibrium steady states by interspersing unitary dynamics with measurements and resets at random times. In spite of this, a quantum hardware validation of such non-equilibrium steady states is still missing. Here, we achieve this goal by first formulating a noisy discrete-time theory where unitary gates alternate with noisy mid-circuit projective measurements and conditional resets. This noisy conditional resetting theory is then demonstrated on a superconducting quantum processor for up to $N=7$ qubits. We consider, as a paradigmatic case, the unitary dynamics of the interacting Floquet transverse-field Ising model. The stationary state of the noisy conditional resetting agrees quantitatively with the experiments, and it shows crossover behavior related to the equilibrium quantum phase transition of the model. Our results might thus pave the way for the preparation of collective stationary states on noisy quantum devices and for further developments of quantum algorithms involving mid-circuit measurements.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计算机有望解决分子电子结构问题，但相关量子算法的性能高度依赖与目标本征态有较大重叠的初始态制备。对于强电子关联的经典难题分子，需要从多参考态（如CAS波函数）出发，然而现有最先进的态制备协议对该类态的门复杂度随活性空间大小d呈指数增长，甚至经典编码CAS态也被认为不可行，因此需要更高效的表示与制备方法。

Method: 借鉴量子Paldu变换（QPT），该变换将Fock基映射到更友好的对称适应基。作者证明在该基下展开的CAS态可高效表示为矩阵乘积态（MPS），键维数标度为O(d²)。随后可将MPS高效加载到量子计算机上，并利用逆QPT将态变换回Fock基。此外，该方法可扩展至第一量子化框架下的CAS态高效制备。

Result: 两种态制备协议的门复杂度均仅为O(d³)的多项式增长，相比现有协议实现了指数级改进。

Conclusion: 该工作为强电子关联分子的量子计算提供了高效的初态制备方案，突破了传统CAS态在经典表示和量子制备上的指数壁垒，具有重要的理论意义和实际应用价值。

Abstract: Quantum computers promise to solve the electronic structure problem for a large class of molecules. However, the performance of relevant quantum algorithms hinges on preparing initial states with substantial overlap with the target eigenvector. For classically challenging molecules with strong electron correlation, starting from multi-reference states, such as complete active space (CAS) wavefunctions is necessary. Unfortunately, the most advanced state preparation protocols applied to such states result in a gate complexity that scales exponentially with the active space size $d$. In fact, even encoding a CAS state classically is traditionally believed to be intractable for chemically relevant systems. Here, we draw insights from the recently introduced Quantum Paldus Transform (QPT) to show that there exists an efficient classical representation of CAS states and to design a new state preparation routine outperforming previous ones. The QPT represents a transformation from the Fock basis to a friendlier symmetry-adapted basis. Our main contribution consists in showing that CAS states expanded in this basis can efficiently be represented as a matrix product state (MPS) with a bond dimension scaling as $O(d^2)$. One can then efficiently load the MPS on a quantum computer and use the inverse QPT to transform the state to the Fock basis. Moreover, our method can easily be extended to the efficient preparation of CAS states in first quantisation with similar complexity. Crucially, we demonstrate that the complexity of both state preparation protocols only grows polynomially as $O(d^3)$ , which constitutes to the best of our knowledge an exponential improvement over the state of the art.

Abstract: This work explores the effects of both the standard quantum $q$-deformation and the non-standard $h$-deformation of the Hopf algebra $\mathcal{U}(\mathfrak{sl}(2, \mathbb{R}))$ on multi-qubit systems. By constructing the states of a Hilbert space of $N$ qubits through the Clebsch-Gordan coefficients associated with the deformed algebras, we show that these states naturally coincide with the eigenstates of the Hamiltonian of the $q$- and $h$-deformed Kittel-Shore models. We compare the resulting deformed states with those typically targeted in quantum information experiments, providing a bridge between algebraic constructions and experimentally relevant quantum resources. Fidelities with respect to the undeformed states are computed to establish how the quantum correlations are affected, both for few-qubit systems (including Dicke and non-Dicke states), and in the macroscopic limit ($N \to \infty$) through closed-form formulas derived for arbitrary Dicke states. The results reveal different behaviors between the two deformations. The $q$-deformation smoothly modifies the states and maintains a residual overlap with the original configurations, while the $h$-deformation rapidly makes the states orthogonal to their undeformed counterparts. Abstract: High-performance quantum low-density parity-check codes promise substantial reductions in the overhead of fault-tolerant quantum computation, but most constructions require long-range connectivity or qubit shuttling, both of which are difficult to realise in superconducting architectures. Here we introduce a family of quantum low-density parity-check codes that, for the first time, combines planar open-boundary layouts, finite-size advantages over surface codes, and syndrome extraction using only nearest-neighbour gates on a square grid of qubits. The key idea is to generate check-data connectivity dynamically: nearest-neighbour iSWAP walks both define the stabiliser supports and implement their measurement, avoiding the need for a long-range hardware graph. The resulting circuits achieve optimal constant-depth stabiliser measurement, independent of code size, and naturally remove leakage from the system by exchanging the role of check and data qubits at each syndrome extraction round. We find finite-size instances such as a [[323,14,15]] code, whose code-efficiency ratio is nearly an order of magnitude larger than that of rotated surface-code patches. At around 30 circuit qubits per logical qubit, the best directional tile-code layouts reduce the per-logical per-round logical error rate by up to a factor of 1000 relative to rotated surface-code memories. These results show that the advantages of quantum low-density parity-check codes can survive compilation into strictly planar nearest-neighbour circuits, bringing low-overhead fault-tolerant memories closer to near-term hardware.

Abstract: Characterizing the features of a Hamiltonian that governs a quantum system serves as a fundamental subroutine of quantum device calibration, signal sensing, and error correction. Recent works proposed protocols have achieved the optimal Heisenberg-limited scaling learning ansatz-free Hamiltonians from their real-time evolutions without fully specifying interaction structures. However, these protocols rely on both deep circuits with interleaving probes and control, and extremely short time resolution, making them difficult to implement on near- and intermediate-term in situ quantum experiments. In this work, we propose a computationally efficient, control-free, and ancilla-free algorithm that uses only Pauli product state preparation and measurement, and learns an ansatz-free Hamiltonian $H$ with $||H||\leqΛ$ in total evolution time of $Θ(\fracΛ{ε^2}\log(\fracΛε))$. The evolution time cost of our algorithm is optimal for any control-free protocols as we further prove a lower bound of $Ω(\fracΛ{ε^2}\log(\fracΛε))$. Technically, our method introduces a randomized-sampling framework that combines band-limited kernel-based time sampling with a displacement sieve for Hamiltonian structure learning. The characteristic probe time resolution depends only on $Λ$ instead of $\varepsilon$, which makes our protocol especially appealing in the high-precision regime for sensing and calibration applications. We also show that the algorithm maintains the same asymptotic total evolution time in the presence of state-preparation-and-measurement (SPAM) noise when the Hamiltonian is local after calibration. Our results demonstrate the fundamental cost of experimentally friendly Hamiltonian learning and provide a practical route to rigorous in situ characterization of near-term quantum platforms.

### [60] [Random Local Stabilizer Codes in Three Dimensions without String or Self-Similar Fractal Logical Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19873)

Abstract: Quantum error-correcting codes (QECs) are essential components quantum computation and have deep connections to quantum phases of matter. A key obstruction to passive self-correcting QECs is the presence of string logical operators, which can generate logical errors through constant-energy-barrier processes. Haah's Codes (fracton codes) showed that three-dimensional stabilizer codes can forbid such string logical operators, but their translation-invariant structure supports self-similar fractal logical operators with a logarithmic energy barrier. We introduce the qutrit random cubic codes, a family of local qutrit Calderbank-Shor-Steane stabilizer Hamiltonians with similar cube-check structure as Haah's Code 1 but built from spatially varying stabilizers. We prove that these models retain the no-string property and numerically observe that they have properties distinct from translation-invariant fracton codes: the smallest ground-state degeneracy exponent is $k=2$ for odd $L$ and $k=4$ for even $L$; noncontractible plane-logical operators span the entire logical space; and charge-push diagnostics show that the self-similar fractal operators are absent. These results demonstrate that constrained randomness can fundamentally change the nature of stabilizer codes and improve their self-correction properties. They further point to broader families of quantum error-correcting codes and quantum phases beyond canonical topological and fracton orders.

### [61] [Quantum Dynamics from Lax Pair Theory: A Reconstruction from Spectrum Preservation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19664)

TL;DR: 本文从最小公理基础重建幺正量子动力学，仅假设可观测量在时间演化中保持谱不变（即测量结果的概率分布不变），由此推导出Lax形式的量子动力学。海森堡方程、薛定谔方程、守恒律和好量子数均作为定理而非公理出现。哈密顿量并非假设，而是作为等谱可观测量流所需的生成元自然涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 试图从更基本的公理出发重建量子动力学，摆脱将哈密顿量作为基本假设的传统框架，仅基于可观测量及其谱的守恒来推导整个量子动力学结构。

Method: 以希尔伯特空间中的可观测量和等谱演化为核心公理，假设物理时间演化是保持可观测量谱（即测量可能结果）的连续单参数流，利用Lax对理论建立可观测量测量结构与标准量子演化之间的动力学桥梁。

Result: 证明了等谱演化假设足以迫使量子动力学呈现Lax形式，海森堡方程、含时与不含时薛定谔方程、守恒律和好量子数均可作为定理推导出来，哈密顿量作为等谱可观测量流所需的生成元自发涌现。

Conclusion: 量子动力学可以从更基本的可观测量谱守恒原理出发被重建，哈密顿量不是基本假设而是推导结果，Lax对理论提供了连接测量结构与量子演化的动力学桥梁。

Abstract: We reconstruct unitary quantum dynamics from a minimal axiomatic foundation built on Hilbert-space observables and isospectral evolution. The only dynamical assumption is that physical time evolution is a continuous one-parameter flow of Hermitian observables that preserves their spectra, i.e. the possible outcomes of measurement. We show that this assumption is already sufficient to force the Lax form of quantum dynamics. The Heisenberg equation, the time-dependent and time-independent Schrödinger equations, conservation laws, and good quantum numbers then follow as theorems rather than postulates. In this formulation, Lax pair theory supplies the missing dynamical bridge between the measurement structure of a Hilbert space and standard quantum evolution: the Hamiltonian is not assumed, but emerges as the generator required for an isospectral observable flow.

Abstract: Entanglement is widely regarded as a key resource underlying the power of quantum algorithms and their potential to achieve quantum advantage. With the emergence of variational quantum algorithms, however, questions have arisen regarding how entanglement relates to problem structure and algorithmic performance in near-term quantum applications. Here, we examine this relationship through the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA), a specific class of variational algorithms, applied to the MaxCut problem. We show that suboptimal variational parameter training can significantly modify the observed entanglement profile, obscuring its scaling behavior. By employing a high-performance optimizer, we find empirical evidence that QAOA exhibits entanglement scaling consistent with that of fermionic Gaussian states (up to a scaling factor) across a broad range of MaxCut instances. We further compare these results with adiabatic quantum computation, observing annealing-schedule-dependent entanglement profiles whose scaling behavior differs markedly from that of QAOA. Together, these findings provide new insight into how entanglement manifests in and distinguishes these two algorithmic paradigms, highlighting its connection to both computational performance and application structure.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过VQE仿真建立现象学模型，将算法精度、资源成本（量子门操作总数）和硬件噪声三者关联起来；考虑量子电路大小（小电路精度不足，大电路噪声过大）与电路迭代次数之间的权衡，使用噪声-度量-资源方法论寻找最优工作点。
